***монополия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:монополия.html>монопо́лия</a> (9582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monopōlium</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">monopolia</i> or New High <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Monopolia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μονοπώλιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monopṓlion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монополия.html>монопо́лия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">monopólija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монополия.html>монопо́лии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монополия.html>монопо́лии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монополия.html>монопо́лий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>monopoly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">various senses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>exclusive domain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Pre-Soviet Russia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a government liquor store</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:монстр.html>монстр</a> (8574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">monstre</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монстр.html>монстр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">monstr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монстр.html>мо́нстра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монстр.html>мо́нстры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монстр.html>мо́нстров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>monster (<i>a terrifying and dangerous creature</i>)</li>
<li>monster, fiend (<i>an evil person</i>)</li></ol>

***монтировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:монтировать.html>монти́ровать</a> (25360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">montieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монтировать.html>монти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">montírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смонтировать.html>смонти́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to assemble <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to put together</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to mount, to arrange (cinema)</li></ol>

***мор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мор.html>мор</a> (14360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">моръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">morŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*morъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́лей</a></b>)

<ol><li>morals; morality

***моральный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:моральный.html>мора́льный</a> (3407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моральный.html>мора́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мора́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мора́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>moral <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to principles of right and wrong</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мо.html>мо</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́ль<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>мора́льнее, мора́льней, помора́льнее, помора́льней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ль</a></b> ➔ <a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ль</a> + <b>н</b> + ый (суффиксальный).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мораль-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***моргать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:моргать.html>морга́ть</a> (10659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mъrgati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моргать.html>морга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morgátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моргнуть.html>моргну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blink
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>гла́зом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:моргнуть.html>моргну́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glázom ne morgnúv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">without batting an eyelid; at a moment's notice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a> кто́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>гла́зом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:моргнуть.html>моргну́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne uspél któ-libo i glázom morgnútʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">before one could bat an eye/eyelid; before one knew it</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wink</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моргнувший.html>моргну́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morgnúvšij</span>)

***морда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рда</a> (1730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iranian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Iranian languages">Iranian</a></span> language, based on the appearance of /r/ in place of /l/; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">molda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">βλωθρός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blōthrós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lifted up, high</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मूर्धन्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mūrdhán</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forehead, head, apex</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬐𐬀-𐬨𐬆𐬭𐬆𐬜𐬀</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ka-mərəδa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-Iranian language">Proto-Indo-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="iir-pro">*mr̥hdʰā́</i>. Possibly connected with synonymous <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Armenian language">Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="hy">մռութ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mṙutʿ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mórda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>face of an animal, muzzle, snout

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face of a person <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually ugly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, mug</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мордашка.html>морда́шка</a> (26040)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">морда́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mordáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cutie, cute face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mórda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">muzzle, snout, mug</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-áška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (sense of "breed of dog" probably derived directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mórda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

***мордобой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мордобой.html>мордобо́й</a> (17514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мордобой.html>мордобо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mordobój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мордобой.html>мордобо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мордобой.html>мордобо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мордобой.html>мордобо́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fist fight, scuffle (the one where people are beaten on the face)</li></ol>

***море.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>море</a> (526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*moře</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*móri</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">marine</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">maritime</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">móre</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>моря́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>море́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́рем</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mórem</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by sea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́рем</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zá morem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overseas</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">и́з-за <b><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ря</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">íz-za <b>mórja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from abroad</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>móre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at sea, at the seaside (location), or to the seaside (direction)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ря</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u <b>mórja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by the seaside</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:открытый.html>откры́тое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otkrýtoje <b>móre</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the high seas</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mare <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">darker area in the Moon</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спокойствие.html>споко́йствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móre Spokójstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mare Tranquillitatis</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:морж.html>морж</a> (21584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi">mursu</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skolt_Sami_language" class="extiw" title="w:Skolt Sami language">Skolt Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sms">moršša</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морж.html>морж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морж.html>моржа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морж.html>моржи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морж.html>морже́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">моржи́ха</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моржовый.html>моржо́вый</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>walrus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> winter swimmer, ice swimmer</li></ol>

***морить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:морить.html>мори́ть</a> (20997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мор.html>мор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морить.html>мори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to kill, to exterminate</li>
<li>to exhaust, to wear out

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>морко́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">morkóvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морковка.html>морко́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морковка.html>морко́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морковка.html>морко́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> carrot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">root vegetable, usually orange</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
